que su pesio hmoi anua se extederet ferre reueret ut ecia eatemis loge retractis torib te pscriptibili ochianos ecclia rum birte citat cosuetu erri terat qd que steutoem hmoi ut pote laudabilem nonulli ei predecessor archiepi cantuarien expresse confirmauer constitucionem ipam quasdam suas litter excerta sua scientia confirmaner et approbauerat et cum non iudli ex ochianis dictum rum ecclia rum suo uerso sensu constitucionem ipam sanu ipius intellectu subuertere tere tur certam desup declarationem fecerat ac maiorem vicicountes que et aldmannos dicte ciuitat necnon ois et singulos ciues seu inhabitantes ea sub pena maio excommicatois cui non patentes et rebelles ipso facto decreuerat subiacere et interminaci one maledictiois eterne monuit quatenus constitucionem et declaratione predictas de cetero ab que sensu peruiso seu corta exposicione inuiolabiliter obseruarent et facerent quantu eis e secitin futuru ab alijs obseruari non nulla quo que alia tunc expressa preceperat factor depittes aforesaid fro euer accion proteccion sauegarde wt let arrest veratio tbauce sau surly suffer go bide go comfro furthermore haue grauntid w thes oure presentis lettres patenns vnto oure clothe kepe wel thing said modur graffyng som men late roete ende vyne vncutt yere til sowded chiritee cut way yt good maner asure soo may doo dyuers tree dyuers frut grape vyne shall haue sauour hem soo euery tree may grraffid meruelous graffyg yf thou haue tree bere u frutis dyuers colour diuers sauaure furst yere graf dyuers brauches cheritree dyuers aples thy lykyng leue braunches vngraffed ij haue true feythfull serua te recommend may please good lordship vnderstonde necessyte hath causeth writte lettre vnto grace moche knowe self ferdful defaute comyng cause knowe self vnworthy haue ony word presence though haue neuer good mater neyther dare shewe wherfore beseche grace rede thise lettre wherby grace shal vnderstonde trouth mater betwene mayster foster yet hanging iugement afore grace myne intollerable cost charge onlesse grace hastely remedyed yf ony thing lettre vntrue contente grace giue vnto therfore perpetuell prison first delyuerd clothes engrened mayster foster delyuer ouer creditours xv l yarde apperith deposicion robert odyam parte mayster foster wher sayth yt sawe mayster foster house lettre ha de wherin conteyned shulde delyuere sayd foster sold iij scarlett yarde ther labor xij cost euery yard xiiij redy money mayster foster wyl alowe lityl aboue v yarde myne vtter vndoyng onles wyll accordynge good conscience myne helpe socoure therfore humbly beseche youre grace euer haue ben true seruaunt power ye suffer nott vntrue dealing sayde foster bee thus vndone euer haue bene ye shal finde youre true feythful seruaunt ihesus kepe grace prosperite amen pthe lawes beleue sarasyns maunduyle wryttyth booke pylgrymage trauayle lawes beleue sarasyns boke callen alcarom callend boke mesaap hem diuers langage dyuers countreys whiche boke machemet made gaue hem whiche wrote amonge thingis iohn mande e haue often red seyn ben good shal goon radyse tho euyl helle trowen sarasyns yf man aske hem paradyse beemeneth sayn place delytis man shall fynde alle maner delytis maner frutis al tymes yuer rennyng mylke wyn ed hony freshe water shal haue fayr house haue deserued house ben made precious stone gold syluer eche shal haue x wynes maydes also speken nowen virgin mary also incarnacion lord ihesu cryste mary lernyd angel gabryel sayde chosen beforne al fro begynyng worlde wytnesse ther booke yt tolde incarnacion ihesu cryst conceyued bare childe yet mayde sayne thu cryste spac sone borne god phere worde dede meke right wi wt n vice sayne whan aungell colde icarnacio drede yong ther delyd myche wt men callid wyth enchauntement owde make lyke au gell rede ofte lay maydens therfore lady aferd wende haungell ben wet maydes therfore lady ferd hi bad hy angell verry aungell messanger lorde criste also booke childe vndir shamed wepte wolde bendede ye childe sayd nerimeas maria say drede mari mother pla booke sath e spak sone borne boke sa k sent lord almyghty ye exaple alle men yt god shal deme good heuyn euill helle crist ye best profight next god verry phet yaf sight blinde helid sels reysed de men steied quyk yf may fynde booke gospel namly ye gospell missus est angelus gabriell gret wurship therto fasten vij monthes yere ete nought nyght kepen hem ther wyues ben lyke costryned fast booke spekith oft iewes sayth yt wyked folke trowe ihu crist oon wyth good seyn iuwes lye lady son ihu crist whan ye seyne dedyn ye crosse sar en trowen soo myche feith lyghtly co uere whan men pchen hem awe crist sey ten well lawe machemet shall faylen dothe lawe iawes crist lawe shal last wordis ende aske hem wheryn trowen yt say god lorde glouceter brought vnto hy freire randolf whiche long befor counfessid treson done hym ayenst kyngis person dede whiche knowleage put kept ye sayd toure straitly comaundid vndir grete payne yeuen sayd scot kepe streitly snerely nott lete hymoute sayd toure wt oute commaundement kyng bi aduise coucell freer randelf mi lorde glouceter kept full hi self weting said scot declared vnto sayd lorde thought lorde wichester sayd lorde glouceter toke hym self ferther autorytee strecchid causid hym doute drede lest wolde haue cedid ferthir monyd hym suche tyme sayd modeuile come onto hym ar aduice
